      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses that will occur in the 27th century
       </b>
       . During the period 2601 to 2700 there will be 227
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 77 will be partial, 81 will be annular (three [4Solar eclipse#Terminology|non-central]]), 64 will be total, and 5 will be hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year will be four, in 7 different years: 2615, 2633, 2644, 2662, 2680, 2691, and 2698. One month, October 2684, will have two eclipses.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
